				<h1 id="firstHeading" class="firstHeading pagetitle page-header">
					Wer mich liebet, der wird mein Wort halten, BWV 74 (Bach, Johann Sebastian)				</h1>	

				<div class="body"><div lang="en" dir="ltr" class="mw-content-ltr"><div class="wp_header">
<table>
<table>

<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Movements/Sections</span><span class="ms555">Mov'ts/Sec's</span>
</th>
<td>8 movements
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Composition Year
</th>
<td>1725 in Leipzig
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Genre Categories<span class="addpagetag mh555"></span>

<h2> <span class="mw-headline" id="Misc._Comments">Misc. Comments</span></h2>
<p>For Whit Sunday.
</p>
<h4> <span class="mw-headline" id="Commentary_on_the_movements">Commentary on the movements</span></h4>
<ol><li>Chorus: Wer mich liebet, der wird mein Wort halten. See Cantata 59/i. This adds an extra trumpet and the oboe chorus. 
</li><li>Aria (Soprano): Konn, komm, mein Herze steht dir offen. See Cantata 59/iv. Bach replaces violin with oboe da caccia, and bass with soprano. 
</li><li>Recitativo (Alto): Die Wohnung ist bereit. Secco recitative. 
</li><li>Aria (Bass): Ich gehe hin und komme wieder zu euch. A continuo aria; <i>basso quasi ostinato</i>. 
</li><li>Aria (Tenor): Kommt, eilet, stimmet Sait und Lieder. The first violin has a virtuosic concertante part here. 
</li><li>Recitativo (Bass): Es ist nichts Verdammliches an denen. Recitative with oboes. 
</li><li>Aria (Alto): Nichts kann mich erretten. A "lively dance-like piece in which the...choirs engage in antiphonal exchanges"<sup>1</sup>. 
</li><li>Chorale: Kein Menschenkind hier auf der Erd. A plain chorale setting. 
</li></ol>
<h4> <span class="mw-headline" id="Print_Sources_Consulted">Print Sources Consulted</span></h4>

</li></ul>
<dl><dd>Oxford: Oxford University Press, 2005.

<ul><li>Cantatas, BWV 221–224
</li></ul>
</th></tr>
<tr>
<td style="background-color: #e6f0f5">
<ul><li> BWV 221: <i>Wer sucht die Pracht, wer wünscht den Glanz</i> (composer unknown}
</li><li> BWV 222: <i>Mein Odem ist schwach</i> (by <a href="/wiki/Category:Bach,_Johann_Ernst" title="Category:Bach, Johann Ernst">Johann Ernst Bach</a>)
</li><li> BWV 223: <i>Meine Seele soll Gott loben</i>
</li><li> BWV 224: <i>Reisst euch los, bekränkte Sinnen</i> (by <a href="/wiki/Category:Bach,_Carl_Philipp_Emanuel" title="Category:Bach, Carl Philipp Emanuel">Carl Philipp Emanuel Bach</a>?)
</li></ul>
</td></tr></table>
